  <script>
   function getQueryParam(paramName) {
        var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
        var params = query.split('&');
        for (var i = 0; i < params.length; i += 1) {
          var pair = params[i].split('=');
          if (pair[0] === paramName) {
            return pair[1];
          }
        }
        return false;
      };
      function removeURLParameter(url, param) {
        var urlParts = url.split('?');
        if (urlParts.length >= 2) {
          var prefix = "".concat(encodeURIComponent(param), "=");
          var params = urlParts[1].split(/[&;]/g);
          for (var i = params.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
            if (params[i].lastIndexOf(prefix, 0) !== -1) {
              params.splice(i, 1);
            }
          }
          url = urlParts[0];
          if (params.length > 0) {
            url += "?".concat(params.join('&'));
          }
          return url;
        }
        return url;
      };
      function setCookie(cookieName, value, daysToExpire) {
        var expires = '';
        if (daysToExpire) {
          var date = new Date();
          date.setTime(date.getTime() + daysToExpire * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
          expires = "; expires=".concat(date.toGMTString());
        }
        if (expires !== '') {
          document.cookie = "".concat(cookieName, "=").concat(value).concat(expires, "; path=/");
        }
        return true;
      };
      (function(){
        var hid = getQueryParam('hid');
        if (!hid) {
          return;
        }
        setCookie('hid', hid, 90);
        window.location.replace(removeURLParameter(window.location.href, 'hid'));
      })();
  </script>

        var cookie = document.cookie.match('(^|;)\\s*' + name + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');

      }

              <div class="media-body article-info bucket-margin margin-24-bottom clearfix">
               <h4 class="headline">
                <a class="heading-3 heading-content margin-8-bottom media-heading headline" data-tracking-label="Explore &gt; 15 Impossible-to-Kill Outdoor Plants" href="https://www.realsimple.com/home-organizing/gardening/outdoor/impossible-to-kill-outdoor-plants">
                 15 Impossible-to-Kill Outdoor Plants
                </a>
               </h4>
               <span class="summary margin-8-bottom">
                With summer in full swing, it&amp;rsquo;s hard not to admire the yards and gardens around town that are filled with greenery and colorful blooms. If you&amp;rsquo;ve always assumed that your yard was too dry, too shady, or that the soil was too sandy to support such beautiful plants&amp;mdash;guess again. In fact, these common problems may just inspire you to get more creative with your plant picks. With expert advice and care tips from a couple of plant pros, we&amp;rsquo;ve ID&amp;rsquo;d 15 pretty plants that will thrive in even the least plant-friendly spaces. Fragrant, flowering dianthus will not only survive in sandy soil, but it will also fill your backyard with color and a lovely, slightly spicy scent. If you have a shady yard that doesn&amp;rsquo;t get much sun, skip the grass and carpet the ground with common oak sedge, which adds textural interest to the area. With these hard-to-kill plants readily available at nurseries and garden centers, there&amp;rsquo;s no reason to let a dry, low-light space stop you from creating a showstopping backyard.

     <h2 class="categoryPageListSixFeatured__title">

     <div class="categoryPageListSixFeatured__main">
      <div class="category-page-item">
